    SELECT `a4`.`Articles_which_dislikedId`, `a4`.`Users_who_dislikedId`, `a5`.`Id`, `a5`.`About`, `a5`.`Created`, `a5`.`Email`, `a5`.`Login`, `a5`.`Name`, `a5`.`Password`, `a5`.`Photo`, `a5`.`Role`, `a5`.`Secret_code`, `a5`.`Surname`, `a5`.`Status_Id`, `a5`.`Status_Status`, `a5`.`Status_Status_text`, `a5`.`Status_Status_title`
    FROM `ArticleUser_account1` AS `a4`
    INNER JOIN `Accounts` AS `a5` ON `a4`.`Users_who_dislikedId` = `a5`.`Id`
) AS `t2` ON `t`.`Id` = `t2`.`Articles_which_dislikedId`
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT `a6`.`Articles_which_been_readId`, `a6`.`Users_who_have_readId`, `a7`.`Id`, `a7`.`About`, `a7`.`Created`, `a7`.`Email`, `a7`.`Login`, `a7`.`Name`, `a7`.`Password`, `a7`.`Photo`, `a7`.`Role`, `a7`.`Secret_code`, `a7`.`Surname`, `a7`.`Status_Id`, `a7`.`Status_Status`, `a7`.`Status_Status_text`, `a7`.`Status_Status_title`
    FROM `ArticleUser_account2` AS `a6`
    INNER JOIN `Accounts` AS `a7` ON `a6`.`Users_who_have_readId` = `a7`.`Id`
) AS `t3` ON `t`.`Id` = `t3`.`Articles_which_been_readId`
LEFT JOIN `Comments` AS `c` ON `t`.`Id` = `c`.`Article_id`
ORDER BY `t`.`Id`, `t0`.`ArticlesId`, `t0`.`AuthorsId`, `t0`.`Id`, `t1`.`Articles_which_likedId`, `t1`.`Users_who_likedId`, `t1`.`Id`, `t2`.`Articles_which_dislikedId`, `t2`.`Users_who_dislikedId`, `t2`.`Id`, `t3`.`Articles_which_been_readId`, `t3`.`Users_who_have_readId`, `t3`.`Id`, `c`.`Id`
Executed DbCommand (1ms) [Parameters=[], CommandType='Text', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT `a`.`Id`, `a`.`Content`, `a`.`Created`, `a`.`Description`, `a`.`Tags`, `a`.`Theme`, `a`.`Title_image`, `a`.`Users_who_have_read_count`
FROM `Articles` AS `a`
